data-reactid="83"><h2>Look Alluring with Beautiful Women's Kurtis from Myntra</h2>
<p>Well-fitted women's kurtis are a great starting piece when stepping into the wonderful world of Indian ethnic wear. Not only are the garments breathtakingly beautiful but come in a large variety of fabrics, thread work, prints, embellishments, designs and fits. You can style them to perfection without much effort. </p>
<p><a class="seolink" href="/kurtas">Kurtas</a> are the traditional garb of choice for both men and women in many parts of southern Asia, including Sri Lanka, Pakistan, India, Bangladesh, Nepal, etc. 'Kurta', in Persian, means a shirt without a collar. Although initially worn by men, it later became popular among women's fashion trends. Women's kurtas that have a shorter length took on a new name—Kurtis.</p>
<p>Whether you like to stick to classic styles or experiment with bold, contemporary designs for a fusion look, Myntra's kurtis collection has it all, and more. Get your hands on the ultimate selection of <a class="seolink" href="/women-ethnic-wear">women's ethnic wear</a> online before stocks run out.</p>
<h2>Find the Perfect Style with Women’s Kurtis Collection Online</h2>
<p>Women from all over the country have worn Kurtis. Let us take a look at the styles you can grab on Myntra. </p>
<li><a href="/designer-kurtis"><strong>Designer Kurtis</strong></a>- Kurtis are a multi-faceted clothing item and can be worn with anything, right from churidars and palazzos to leggings and jeans. Whether you love sporting cotton kurtis to work every day or are fond of silk, crepe, georgette or even wool variants for special occasions, is a matter of personal choice. Shop for hand and block printed pieces to embroidered items with beads, sequins and stones.</li>
<li><strong>Kurti Sets</strong>- Sky's the limit when styling your favourite <a class="seolink" href="/salwar-suit">designer salwar suit</a>, and the same applies to kurti sets. Wear our women’s kurtis collection one way today and another way tomorrow. Show your creativity as much as possible. No matter what the occasion, your style or budget, our Palazzo kurti sets will impress you to no end.</li>
<h2>Tips on Experimenting with Women’s Kurtis on Myntra</h2>
<p>Here are a few of our style recommendations when shopping for women’s kurtis on Myntra.</p>
<li>Try women’s kurtis in bright, solid colours like fluorescent green or fiery red and a buttoned front placket coupled up with roll-up sleeves. These can easily pair with jeggings in a complementary colour and ballet flats.</li>
<li>Choose cotton kurtis with simple embroidered detail against a light colour background and asymmetric hem. Pair them with distressed jeans and oversized sunglasses for a fun but practical look that will delight both you and your pals. </li>
<li>Beat the summer heat in sleeveless chikankari women’s kurtis in pastel colours. Pair them with white palazzos and open sandals for a look that will keep you feeling cool.</li>
<li>Switch up your <a class="seolink" href="/patiala-suits">designer Patiala suits</a> with lightweight kurtis and jeans combination. Alternate the bottoms with harem pants in vibrant colours. Carry a large leather handbag to bring the look together.</li>
